*** Tests the DIFFERENCE in performance when using different ALPHA ADJUSTMENT values



*** NOTES ***
    - Absolute values should obviously not be taken seriously, but just as a comparison.
    - Alpha Adjustment Values is chosen such that alpha is adjusted by that amount at 50% recall probability



*** TEST SETTINGS ***
Learn sessions         = 50
Immediate alpha adjust = True
Alpha adjust value     = 0.02
Cache used             = True
Cache updated          = post-session
